genecounts <- featureCounts(files = bam_files,
                            annot.ext = annot_file,
                          isGTFAnnotationFile = TRUE,
                            isPairedEnd= TRUE)

# Create DESeq dataset from the count matrix

                              colData = colData,
                              design = ~Treatment+ Gender+ Treatment:Gender)

# Get results and order the tables
#Treatment
dds_results_treatment <- results(object = dds,
                       contrast = c("Treatment", "4-AP", "ACSF" ))

dds_results_treatment <- dds_results_treatment[order(abs(dds_results_treatment$log2FoldChange), decreasing = TRUE, na.last = TRUE), ]

#Gender
dds_results_gender <- results(object = dds,
                       contrast = c("Gender", "Male", "Female" ))

dds_results_gender <- dds_results_gender[order(abs(dds_results_gender$log2FoldChange), decreasing = TRUE, na.last = TRUE), ]

#Interacting Factor
dds_results_interaction <- results(object = dds,
                       name = c("Treatment4.AP.GenderMale" ))

dds_results_interaction <- dds_results_interaction[order(abs(dds_results_interaction$log2FoldChange), decreasing = TRUE, na.last = TRUE), ]
